- mixture-models ‚Äîuses‚Üí dirichlet-distribution
- mixture-models ‚Äîapplies‚Üí clustering
- gaussian-mixture-models ‚Äîuses‚Üí gibbs-sampler
- gaussian-mixture-models ‚Äîuses‚Üí dirichlet-distribution
- gaussian-mixture-models ‚Äîapplies‚Üí number-of-components-selection
